jawaharlal nehru first prime minister india first convocation iit kharagpur clarified address institutes technology would help meet technological challenges nation
four iits established bombay delhi kanpur madras
subsequently september parliament india passed act known institutes technology act declaring iit kharagpur institute national importance
iit kharagpur given status autonomous university
thereafter iit guwahati started university roorkee given status iit called iit roorkee
establishment eight iits across country began decision cabinet announced minister human resource development march
